##### **DeepTumorVQA: A Hierarchical 3D CT Benchmark for Stage-Wise Evaluation of Medical VLMs and Tool-Augmented Agents**
2605.09679v1 by Yixiong Chen, Wenjie Xiao, Pedro R. A. S. Bassi, Boyan Wang, Liang He, Xinze Zhou, Sezgin Er, Ibrahim Ethem Hamamci, Zongwei Zhou, Alan Yuille

Medical vision-language models (VLMs) and AI agents have made significant progress in learning to analyze and reason about clinical images. However, existing medical visual question answering (VQA) benchmarks collapse model capabilities into a single accuracy score, obscuring where and why models fail. We propose DeepTumorVQA, a hierarchical benchmark that follows the multi-stage evidence chain in tumor diagnosis and decomposes 3D CT reasoning into four stages: recognition, measurement, visual reasoning, and medical reasoning. Higher-level questions remain independently scorable, while their ground-truth evidence chains are defined over lower-level primitives. The benchmark contains 476K questions across 42 clinical subtypes on 9,262 3D CT volumes. In addition to a direct reasoning mode for VLMs, DeepTumorVQA provides tool-interaction environments for agent evaluation, where a model can call external tools, including segmentation models, measurement programs, and medical knowledge modules, before answering the question. Evaluating over 30 model configurations, we find that reliable quantitative measurement is the primary bottleneck, making later-stage visual and medical reasoning harder for VLMs, while tool augmentation substantially mitigates this issue. When tools are available, leveraging medical knowledge and tools to reason about medical images becomes a new challenge. We further show that ground-truth step-by-step tool-use traces from DeepTumorVQA can supervise agents and reduce tool-use and reasoning failures. This stage-wise progression from recognition to measurement to visual and medical reasoning provides a concrete roadmap for future medical VLM and AI agent studies. All data and code are released at https://github.com/Schuture/DeepTumorVQA.

摘要：醫療視覺語言模型 (VLMs) 和 AI 代理在學習分析和推理臨床影像方面取得了顯著進展。<lb/>然而，現有的醫療視覺問題回答 (VQA) 基準將模型能力壓縮為單一的準確度分數，模糊了模型失敗的原因和位置。<lb/>我們提出了 DeepTumorVQA，一個層級基準，遵循腫瘤診斷中的多階段證據鏈，並將 3D CT 推理分解為四個階段：識別、測量、視覺推理和醫學推理。<lb/>高階問題仍然可以獨立評分，而它們的真實證據鏈則在低階原始資料上定義。<lb/>該基準包含 476K 問題，涵蓋 42 種臨床亞型，基於 9,262 份 3D CT 體積。<lb/>除了 VLMs 的直接推理模式外，DeepTumorVQA 還提供了工具互動環境以進行代理評估，模型可以在回答問題之前調用外部工具，包括分割模型、測量程序和醫學知識模塊。<lb/>在評估超過 30 種模型配置後，我們發現可靠的定量測量是主要瓶頸，這使得後階段的視覺和醫學推理對 VLMs 來說更加困難，而工具增強則大大減輕了這一問題。<lb/>當工具可用時，利用醫學知識和工具來推理醫療影像成為一個新的挑戰。<lb/>我們進一步顯示，DeepTumorVQA 的真實逐步工具使用痕跡可以監督代理並減少工具使用和推理失敗。<lb/>從識別到測量再到視覺和醫學推理的這一階段性進展為未來的醫療 VLM 和 AI 代理研究提供了一個具體的路線圖。<lb/>所有數據和代碼已發布於 https://github.com/Schuture/DeepTumorVQA。

##### **CodeClinic: Evaluating Automation of Coding Skills for Clinical Reasoning Agents**
2605.09675v1 by Timothy Ossowski, Xinchi Liu, Danyal Maqbool, Vaibhav Dhanuka, Sheng Zhang, Hoifung Poon, Majid Afshar, Tyler Bradshaw, Junjie Hu

Clinical reasoning agents based on large language models (LLMs) aim to automate tasks such as intensive care unit (ICU) monitoring and patient state tracking from electronic health records (EHRs). Existing systems typically rely on manually curated clinical tools or skills for concepts such as sepsis detection and organ failure assessment. However, maintaining these tool libraries requires substantial expert effort, while zero-shot querying or code generation often produces inefficient and unreliable reasoning chains, especially under institution-specific clinical policies. We introduce CodeClinic, a benchmark built on MIMIC-IV for evaluating whether LLM agents can synthesize and compose reusable clinical skills instead of relying on fixed toolboxes. The benchmark contains two complementary tasks: longitudinal ICU surveillance and compositional information seeking. The longitudinal setting simulates monitoring patient trajectories with structured decisions every four hours across 25 findings and eight clinical families, while the compositional setting spans 63k instances across 259 tasks in nine domains and is stratified by compositional dependency depth to evaluate increasingly complex multi-step reasoning. We further propose an offline autoformalization pipeline that converts natural-language clinical guidelines into reusable and verified Python skill libraries through iterative LLM refinement. Compared with zero-shot code generation, the resulting libraries improve consistency while reducing per-query token usage by up to 40%.

摘要：臨床推理代理基於大型語言模型（LLMs），旨在自動化任務，例如重症監護病房（ICU）監控和從電子健康紀錄（EHRs）中追蹤患者狀態。現有系統通常依賴手動策劃的臨床工具或技能來處理諸如敗血症檢測和器官衰竭評估等概念。然而，維護這些工具庫需要大量專家的努力，而零-shot 查詢或代碼生成往往會產生低效且不可靠的推理鏈，特別是在特定機構的臨床政策下。我們介紹了 CodeClinic，一個基於 MIMIC-IV 的基準，用於評估 LLM 代理是否能合成和組合可重用的臨床技能，而不是依賴固定的工具箱。該基準包含兩個互補的任務：縱向 ICU 監測和組合信息尋求。縱向設置模擬每四小時對 25 個發現和八個臨床家族的結構化決策進行患者軌跡監控，而組合設置則涵蓋了 63k 實例，跨越 259 個任務，並根據組合依賴深度進行分層，以評估日益複雜的多步推理。我們進一步提出了一個離線自動形式化管道，通過迭代的 LLM 精煉將自然語言臨床指導轉換為可重用和經過驗證的 Python 技能庫。與零-shot 代碼生成相比，生成的庫提高了一致性，同時將每次查詢的標記使用量減少了多達 40%。

##### **MedMeta: A Benchmark for LLMs in Synthesizing Meta-Analysis Conclusion from Medical Studies**
2605.09661v1 by Huy Hoang Ha, Benoit Favre, Francois Portet

Large language models (LLMs) have saturated standard medical benchmarks that test factual recall, yet their ability to perform higher-order reasoning, such as synthesizing evidence from multiple sources, remains critically under-explored. To address this gap, we introduce MedMeta, the first benchmark designed to evaluate an LLM's ability to generate conclusions from medical meta-analyses using only the abstracts of cited studies. MedMeta comprises 81 meta-analyses from PubMed (2018--2025) and evaluates models using two distinct workflows: a Retrieval-Augmented Generation (Golden-RAG) setting with ground-truth abstracts, and a Parametric-only approach relying on internal knowledge. Our evaluation framework is validated by a well-structured analysis showing our LLM-as-a-judge protocol strongly aligns with human expert ratings, as evidenced by high Pearson's r correlation (0.81) and Bland-Altman analysis revealing negligible systematic bias, establishing it as a reliable proxy for scalable evaluation. Our findings underscore the critical importance of information grounding: the Golden-RAG workflow consistently and significantly outperforms the Parametric-only approach across models. In contrast, the benefits of domain-specific fine-tuning are marginal and largely neutralized when external material is provided. Furthermore, stress tests show that all models, regardless of architecture, fail to identify and reject negated evidence, highlighting a critical vulnerability in current RAG systems. Notably, even under ideal RAG conditions, current LLMs achieve only slightly above-average performance (~2.7/5.0). MedMeta provides a challenging new benchmark for evidence synthesis and demonstrates that for clinical applications, developing robust RAG systems is a more promising direction than model specialization alone.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）已經在測試事實回憶的標準醫學基準中達到了飽和，然而它們進行高階推理的能力，例如從多個來源綜合證據，仍然嚴重未被探索。為了解決這一空白，我們推出了 MedMeta，這是第一個旨在評估 LLM 從醫學元分析中僅使用引用研究的摘要生成結論能力的基準。MedMeta 包含來自 PubMed（2018--2025）的 81 個元分析，並使用兩種不同的工作流程來評估模型：一種是帶有真實摘要的檢索增強生成（Golden-RAG）設置，另一種是僅依賴內部知識的參數化方法。我們的評估框架通過一個結構良好的分析得到了驗證，顯示我們的 LLM 作為評判者的協議與人類專家的評分高度一致，這一點通過高皮爾森相關係數（0.81）和布蘭德-阿特曼分析顯示的微不足道的系統性偏差得以證明，確立了其作為可擴展評估的可靠代理。我們的發現強調了信息基礎的重要性：Golden-RAG 工作流程在模型中始終顯著地優於僅參數化的方法。相比之下，當提供外部材料時，特定領域的微調所帶來的好處是微不足道的，並在很大程度上被中和。此外，壓力測試顯示，所有模型無論架構如何，都無法識別和拒絕否定的證據，這突顯了當前 RAG 系統的一個關鍵脆弱性。值得注意的是，即使在理想的 RAG 條件下，當前的 LLM 也僅達到略高於平均的表現（約 2.7/5.0）。MedMeta 提供了一個具有挑戰性的證據綜合新基準，並表明對於臨床應用，開發穩健的 RAG 系統比僅僅專注於模型專業化更具前景。

##### **Any2Any 3D Diffusion Models with Knowledge Transfer: A Radiotherapy Planning Study**
2605.09622v1 by Yuhan Wang, Zihan Li, Han Liu, Simon Arberet, Martin Kraus, Yuyin Zhou, Florin-Cristian Ghesu, Dorin Comaniciu, Ali Kamen, Riqiang Gao

Voxel-wise dose prediction is a critical yet challenging task in practical radiotherapy (RT) planning, as bespoke models trained from scratch often struggle to generalize across diverse clinical settings. Meanwhile, generative models trained on billion-scale datasets from vision domains have achieved impressive performance. Herein, we propose DiffKT3D, a unified Any2Any 3D diffusion framework that leverages prior knowledge from pretrained video diffusion models for efficient and clinically meaningful dose prediction. To enable flexible conditioning across multiple clinical modalities (CT, anatomical structures, body, beam settings, etc.), we introduce an Any2Any conditional paradigm utilizing modality-specific embeddings without cross-attention overhead. Further, we design a novel reinforcement learning (RL) post-training mechanism guided by a clinically-informed Scorecard explicitly tailored to institutional treatment preferences. Compared with winner of GDP-HMM challenge, DiffKT3D sets a new state-of-the-art in dose prediction by reducing voxel-level MAE from 2.07 to 1.93. In addition, DiffKT3D achieves superior image quality and preference match. These results demonstrate that transferring diffusion priors via modality-aware conditioning and clinically aligned RL post-training can provide a robust and generalizable solution for RT planning across various clinical scenarios.

摘要：體素級劑量預測是實際放射治療（RT）計劃中一項關鍵但具有挑戰性的任務，因為從零開始訓練的專用模型往往難以在多樣的臨床環境中進行泛化。與此同時，基於視覺領域的十億級數據集訓練的生成模型已經取得了令人印象深刻的表現。在此，我們提出了DiffKT3D，一個統一的Any2Any 3D擴散框架，利用預訓練視頻擴散模型的先驗知識，以實現高效且具有臨床意義的劑量預測。為了在多種臨床模態（CT、解剖結構、身體、束設置等）之間實現靈活的條件設置，我們引入了一種Any2Any條件範式，利用特定模態的嵌入而無需交叉注意力的開銷。此外，我們設計了一種新的強化學習（RL）後訓練機制，該機制由明確針對機構治療偏好的臨床知情評分卡指導。與GDP-HMM挑戰賽的獲勝者相比，DiffKT3D在劑量預測中創造了新的最先進技術，將體素級MAE從2.07降低到1.93。此外，DiffKT3D在圖像質量和偏好匹配方面也表現出色。這些結果表明，通過模態感知條件和與臨床對齊的RL後訓練轉移擴散先驗，可以為各種臨床場景中的RT計劃提供一個穩健且可泛化的解決方案。

##### **CLR-voyance: Reinforcing Open-Ended Reasoning for Inpatient Clinical Decision Support with Outcome-Aware Rubrics**
2605.09584v1 by Aishik Nagar, Arun-Kumar Kaliya-Perumal, Yu-Hsuan Han, Andrew Sheng-Han Huang, Kristen Kee, Yushi Cao, Yiming Chen, Hongchao Jiang

Inpatient clinical reasoning is a sequential decision under partial observability: the clinician sees the admission so far and must choose the next action whose downstream consequences are not yet visible. Existing clinical-LLM evaluations and RL rewards signals collapse this into closed-form retrieval, clinical journey leakage, or unanchored LLM-as-judge scoring. We introduce CLR-voyance, a framework that reformulates inpatient reasoning as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) and supervises it with rewards that are simultaneously outcome-grounded and clinician-validated. We instantiate the formulation as CLR-POMDP, which partitions successful patient journeys into a policy-visible past and an oracle-only future. Using the past information, an oracle LLM generates a case-specific query-answer pair, and the first adaptive rubric for clinical reasoning which is verifiable in the future of the patient journey. These rubrics are used for both post-training and evaluation of models for inpatient clinical reasoning. We post-train Qwen3-8B and MedGemma-4B with GRPO followed by model merging, yielding state-of-the-art inpatient clinical reasoning while retaining generalist capabilities. CLR-voyance-8B achieves 84.91% on CLR-POMDP, ahead of frontier medical reasoning models like GPT-5 (77.83%) and MedGemma-27B (66.66%) and has comparable or better performance on existing medical benchmarks. To ensure a clinically meaningful setting, we conduct a large-scale clinician alignment study, where physicians curate per-case rubrics, grade candidate responses, and provide blinded pairwise preferences of model reasoning. This study provides insights on clinical LLM-as-a-judge and clinical preference-model selection, which can inform the community at large. CLR-voyance has been deployed for 6+ months at a partner public hospital, drafting thousands of reasoning-heavy inpatient notes.

摘要：住院臨床推理是在部分可觀察性下的序列決策：臨床醫生看到目前的入院情況，必須選擇下一個行動，而其後果尚不可見。現有的臨床LLM評估和強化學習獎勵信號將其簡化為封閉形式檢索、臨床旅程泄漏或無錨LLM作為評判的打分。我們提出CLR-voyance，一個將住院推理重新表述為部分可觀察馬爾可夫決策過程（POMDP）的框架，並用同時基於結果和臨床醫生驗證的獎勵進行監督。我們將這一表述具體化為CLR-POMDP，將成功的患者旅程劃分為政策可見的過去和僅限於神諭的未來。利用過去的信息，一個神諭LLM生成一個特定案例的查詢-回答對，以及第一個可在患者旅程的未來驗證的臨床推理自適應評分標準。這些評分標準用於住院臨床推理模型的後訓練和評估。我們使用GRPO對Qwen3-8B和MedGemma-4B進行後訓練，然後進行模型合併，實現了最先進的住院臨床推理，同時保留了通用能力。CLR-voyance-8B在CLR-POMDP上達到84.91%，領先於前沿醫學推理模型，如GPT-5（77.83%）和MedGemma-27B（66.66%），並在現有醫學基準上具有可比或更好的表現。為了確保臨床意義的設置，我們進行了一項大規模的臨床醫生對齊研究，醫生們為每個案例策劃評分標準，對候選回應進行評分，並提供模型推理的盲配對偏好。這項研究為臨床LLM作為評判者和臨床偏好模型選擇提供了見解，這可以為整個社區提供信息。CLR-voyance已在合作的公立醫院部署超過6個月，撰寫了數千份以推理為重的住院筆記。

##### **Biosignal Fingerprinting: A Cross-Modal PPG-ECG Foundation Model**
2605.09579v1 by Zhangdaihong Liu, Chang Liu, Fenglin Liu, Yixuan Chen, Yang Yang, David A. Clifton, Xiao Gu

Cardiovascular disease remains the leading cause of global mortality, yet scalable cardiac monitoring is hindered by the gap between diagnostic-rich ECG and ubiquitous wearable PPG. Bridging this gap requires representations that are compact, transferable across modalities and devices, and deployable without task-specific retraining. Here we introduce biosignal fingerprints: compact latent representations of cardiovascular state derived from a cross-modal foundation model, the Multi-modal Masked Autoencoder (M2AE), trained on over 3.4 million paired ECG and PPG signals. M2AE integrates modality-specific encoders with a shared bottleneck and dual decoders, jointly optimized using reconstruction and cross-modal contrastive objectives, yielding generalizable fingerprints that retain intra- and inter-modality features. Like a biometric fingerprint, these representations uniquely encode an individual's cardiovascular state in a modality-agnostic, privacy-preserving form reusable across clinical tasks without exposing raw waveform data or requiring model retraining. Across 7 downstream tasks, spanning cross-modal reconstruction, cardiovascular disease classification, hypertension detection, mortality prediction, and demographic inference, biosignal fingerprints achieve competitive or superior performance compared to leading domain-specialist foundation models in frozen settings, including an AUROC of 0.974 for five-class CVD classification and 0.877 for hypertension detection, with a maximum improvement of 27.7% in AUROC across 5 classification tasks. Critically, strong performance is maintained with only a single modality, enabling deployment in resource-constrained, single-sensor environments typical of real-world wearable monitoring, with direct implications for continuous cardiovascular monitoring across clinical and consumer health settings.

摘要：心血管疾病仍然是全球死亡的主要原因，但可擴展的心臟監測受到診斷豐富的心電圖（ECG）與無處不在的光電容積描記（PPG）之間的差距所阻礙。彌補這一差距需要緊湊的表示，這些表示能夠跨模態和設備轉移，並且可以在不進行特定任務重新訓練的情況下部署。在這裡，我們介紹生物信號指紋：這是一種來自跨模態基礎模型的心血管狀態的緊湊潛在表示，該模型是多模態掩碼自編碼器（M2AE），其訓練基於超過340萬對的ECG和PPG信號。M2AE整合了特定模態的編碼器，並具有共享的瓶頸和雙解碼器，通過重建和跨模態對比目標進行聯合優化，產生可泛化的指紋，保留了模態內和模態間的特徵。就像生物識別指紋一樣，這些表示以模態無關、保護隱私的形式獨特地編碼個體的心血管狀態，可重複使用於臨床任務，而無需暴露原始波形數據或進行模型重新訓練。在7個下游任務中，涵蓋跨模態重建、心血管疾病分類、高血壓檢測、死亡率預測和人口推斷，生物信號指紋在冷凍設置中實現了與領先的領域專家基礎模型相比具有競爭力或更優的性能，包括五類心血管疾病分類的AUROC為0.974和高血壓檢測的AUROC為0.877，在5個分類任務中AUROC的最大改進達到27.7%。關鍵是，即使僅使用單一模態，強大的性能也得以維持，這使得在資源受限的單傳感器環境中部署成為可能，這在現實世界可穿戴監測中是典型的，對於臨床和消費者健康設置中的持續心血管監測具有直接的影響。

##### **EpiGraph: A Knowledge Graph and Benchmark for Evidence-Intensive Reasoning in Epilepsy**
2605.09505v1 by Yuyang Dai, Zheng Chen, Jathurshan Pradeepkumar, Yasuko Matsubara, Jimeng Sun, Yasushi Sakurai, Yushun Dong

Epilepsy diagnosis and treatment require evidence-intensive reasoning across heterogeneous clinical knowledge, including biosignal patterns, genetic mechanisms, pharmacogenomics, treatment strategies, and patient outcomes. In this work, we present \textsc{EpiGraph}, a large-scale epilepsy knowledge graph and benchmark for evaluating knowledge-augmented clinical reasoning. \textsc{EpiGraph} integrates 48,166 peer-reviewed papers and seven clinical resources into a heterogeneous graph containing 24,324 entities and 32,009 evidence-grounded triplets across five clinical layers. Built upon this graph, \textsc{EpiBench} defines five clinically motivated tasks spanning clinical decision-making, EEG report generation, pharmacogenomic precision medicine, treatment recommendation, and deep research planning. We evaluate six LLMs under both standard and Graph-RAG settings. Results show that integrating \textsc{EpiGraph} consistently improves performance across all tasks, with the largest gains observed in pharmacogenomic reasoning (+30--41\%). Our findings demonstrate that structured epilepsy knowledge substantially enhances evidence-grounded clinical reasoning and provides a practical benchmark framework for evaluating knowledge-augmented LLMs in real-world neurological settings. Our code is available at: https://github.com/LabRAI/EEG-KG.

摘要：癲癇的診斷和治療需要在異質的臨床知識中進行以證據為基礎的推理，包括生物信號模式、遺傳機制、藥物基因組學、治療策略和患者結果。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們呈現了 \textsc{EpiGraph}，這是一個大規模的癲癇知識圖譜和用於評估知識增強臨床推理的基準。<lb/> \textsc{EpiGraph} 將 48,166 篇經過同行評審的論文和七個臨床資源整合到一個異質圖中，該圖包含 24,324 個實體和 32,009 個基於證據的三元組，跨越五個臨床層次。<lb/>基於這個圖，\textsc{EpiBench} 定義了五個臨床驅動的任務，涵蓋臨床決策、腦電圖報告生成、藥物基因組精準醫療、治療建議和深度研究規劃。<lb/>我們在標準和 Graph-RAG 設定下評估了六個 LLM。<lb/>結果顯示，整合 \textsc{EpiGraph} 一致性地提高了所有任務的性能，藥物基因組推理的增益最大（+30--41\%）。<lb/>我們的研究結果表明，結構化的癲癇知識顯著增強了基於證據的臨床推理，並提供了一個實用的基準框架，用於評估現實世界神經學環境中知識增強的 LLM。<lb/>我們的代碼可在以下網址獲得：https://github.com/LabRAI/EEG-KG。

##### **Key Coverage Matters: Semi-Structured Extraction of OCR Clinical Reports**
2605.09440v1 by Yu Wang, Yingyun Li, Ying Qin, Haiyang Qian

Clinical reports are often fragmented across healthcare institutions because privacy regulations and data silos limit direct information sharing. When patients seek care at a different hospital, they often carry paper or scanned reports from prior visits. This hinders EHR integration and longitudinal review, and downstream applications that depend on more complete patient records, such as patient management, follow-up care, real-world studies, and clinical-trial matching. Although OCR can digitize such reports, reliable extraction remains challenging because clinical documents are heterogeneous, OCR text is noisy, and many healthcare settings require low-cost on-premise deployment. We formulate this problem as canonical key-conditioned extractive question answering over OCR-derived clinical reports. Because the key fields are neither fixed nor known in advance, the key space is open. We maintain a canonical key inventory through iterative key mining, normalization, clustering, and lightweight human verification, and introduce key coverage as a metric to quantify inventory completeness. Using a 0.2B BERT-based model, experiments on real-world reports from more than 20 hospitals show performance improves monotonically with key coverage. The model achieves F1 scores of 0.839 and 0.893 under exact match and boundary-tolerant matching, respectively, once the Top-90 canonical keys are covered. These results show that key coverage is a dominant factor for end-to-end performance. At Top-90 coverage, our model outperforms a fine-tuned Qwen3-0.6B baseline under exact match. Although our annotated corpus is Chinese, the method relies on the language-agnostic key-value organization of semi-structured clinical reports and can be adapted to other settings given an appropriate canonical key inventory and alias mapping.

摘要：臨床報告在醫療機構之間往往是支離破碎的，因為隱私法規和數據孤島限制了直接的信息共享。當患者在不同的醫院尋求護理時，他們經常攜帶之前就診的紙本或掃描報告。這阻礙了電子健康記錄（EHR）的整合和縱向審查，以及依賴更完整患者記錄的下游應用，例如患者管理、後續護理、真實世界研究和臨床試驗匹配。儘管光學字符識別（OCR）可以數字化這些報告，但可靠的提取仍然具有挑戰性，因為臨床文件是異質的，OCR文本是嘈雜的，並且許多醫療環境需要低成本的本地部署。我們將這個問題表述為基於關鍵條件的經典提取式問題回答，針對OCR衍生的臨床報告。由於關鍵字段既不是固定的，也不是事先已知的，因此關鍵空間是開放的。我們通過迭代的關鍵挖掘、標準化、聚類和輕量級人類驗證來維護經典關鍵庫，並引入關鍵覆蓋作為量化庫完整性的指標。使用一個0.2B的基於BERT的模型，對來自20多家醫院的真實報告進行的實驗顯示，隨著關鍵覆蓋的增加，性能單調提升。當Top-90經典關鍵被覆蓋時，模型在精確匹配和邊界容忍匹配下分別達到0.839和0.893的F1分數。這些結果顯示，關鍵覆蓋是端到端性能的主導因素。在Top-90覆蓋下，我們的模型在精確匹配下超越了微調的Qwen3-0.6B基準。儘管我們的註釋語料庫是中文，但該方法依賴於半結構化臨床報告的語言無關的鍵值組織，並且可以在給定適當的經典關鍵庫和別名映射的情況下適應其他環境。

##### **LiteMedCoT-VL: Parameter-Efficient Adaptation for Medical Visual Question Answering**
2605.09384v1 by Runze Ma, Shunbo Jia, Haonan Lyu, Guo Liu, Caizhi Liao

The reasoning gap between large and compact vision-language models (VLMs) limits the deployment of medical AI on portable clinical devices. Compact VLMs of 2--4B parameters can run on resource-constrained hardware but lack the multi-step reasoning capacity needed for interpretable clinical decision support. Existing knowledge distillation methods transfer answers without the reasoning process behind them. Medical visual question answering (VQA) serves as a testbed for this problem, as it requires models to integrate visual evidence with clinical knowledge through structured reasoning chains. We introduce LiteMedCoT-VL, a pipeline that transfers chain-of-thought reasoning from a 235B teacher model to 2B student models through LoRA-based fine-tuning on explanation-enriched training data. All inference is conducted without image captions by default, simulating the clinical scenario in which a physician interprets a medical image directly without an accompanying radiology report. On the PMC-VQA benchmark, LiteMedCoT-VL achieves 64.9% accuracy, exceeding the zero-shot Qwen3-VL-4B baseline of 53.9% by 11.0 percentage points and outperforming all published baselines. This result indicates that a 2B model with reasoning distillation can match or exceed models with twice the parameters. Visual grounding analysis shows that the model relies on image content rather than exploiting textual priors. Our code is publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/LiteMedCoT-VL.

摘要：大型與緊湊型視覺語言模型（VLMs）之間的推理差距限制了醫療AI在便攜式臨床設備上的部署。擁有2至4億參數的緊湊型VLM可以在資源受限的硬體上運行，但缺乏可解釋的臨床決策支持所需的多步推理能力。現有的知識蒸餾方法僅轉移答案，而未考慮其背後的推理過程。醫療視覺問題回答（VQA）作為此問題的測試平台，因為它要求模型通過結構化推理鏈整合視覺證據與臨床知識。我們介紹了LiteMedCoT-VL，這是一個將235B教師模型的思維鏈推理轉移到2B學生模型的流程，通過基於LoRA的微調在增強解釋的訓練數據上進行。所有推理默認情況下不進行圖像標題，模擬醫生直接解釋醫療影像而不附帶放射學報告的臨床場景。在PMC-VQA基準上，LiteMedCoT-VL達到了64.9%的準確率，超過了53.9%的零樣本Qwen3-VL-4B基線11.0個百分點，並且超越了所有已發表的基線。這一結果表明，具有推理蒸餾的2B模型可以匹配或超越參數數量為兩倍的模型。視覺基礎分析顯示該模型依賴於圖像內容，而不是利用文本先驗。我們的代碼可在 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/LiteMedCoT-VL 上公開獲取。

##### **Towards a Virtual Neuroscientist: Autonomous Neuroimaging Analysis via Multi-Agent Collaboration**
2605.09366v1 by Keqi Han, Songlin Zhao, Yao Su, Lifang He, Carl Yang

Transforming neuroimaging data into clinically actionable biomarkers is a knowledge-intensive and labor-intensive process. Standardized workflows such as fMRIPrep have improved robustness and efficiency, but they are statically configured and cannot reason about downstream objectives, deliberate over alternative strategies, or close the loop between intermediate evidence and subsequent decisions in the way a human researcher would. This lack of closed-loop adaptation often leaves domain experts trapped in a cycle of manual trial-and-error to tune parameters and remediate pipeline failures, severely constraining the scalability of clinical biomarker development. To bridge this gap, we introduce NIAgent, a multi-agent system for autonomous end-to-end neuroimaging analysis. Unlike conventional flat tool-calling agents, NIAgent adopts a code-centric execution paradigm where specialist agents collaboratively synthesize and optimize executable programs over composable domain-specific primitives. This design enables robust, long-horizon workflow construction that adapts dynamically to runtime observations. Furthermore, we propose a hierarchical verification framework for autonomous quality control, integrating cohort-level metric screening with agentic visual inspection to drive evidence-grounded workflow remediation. Experiments on ADHD-200 and ADNI demonstrate that NIAgent outperforms standard workflow-based baselines in predictive performance while exhibiting sophisticated agentic behaviors, including strategy exploration and adaptive refinement.

摘要：將神經影像數據轉化為臨床可行的生物標記是一個知識密集且勞動密集的過程。標準化工作流程如 fMRIPrep 提高了穩健性和效率，但它們是靜態配置的，無法對下游目標進行推理、考慮替代策略或像人類研究者一樣在中間證據和後續決策之間閉合循環。這種缺乏閉環適應的情況常常使領域專家陷入手動試錯的循環中，以調整參數和修復管道故障，嚴重限制了臨床生物標記開發的可擴展性。為了彌補這一差距，我們引入了 NIAgent，一個用於自主端到端神經影像分析的多代理系統。與傳統的平面工具調用代理不同，NIAgent 採用以代碼為中心的執行範式，專家代理協同合成和優化可執行程序，基於可組合的特定領域原語。這一設計使得能夠構建穩健的長期工作流程，並根據運行時觀察進行動態調整。此外，我們提出了一個層級驗證框架，用於自主質量控制，將群體級別的指標篩選與代理的視覺檢查相結合，以推動基於證據的工作流程修正。在 ADHD-200 和 ADNI 上的實驗表明，NIAgent 在預測性能上優於基於標準工作流程的基準，同時展現出複雜的代理行為，包括策略探索和自適應精煉。

##### **Towards Conversational Medical AI with Eyes, Ears and a Voice**
2605.09272v1 by Meet Shah, Jason Gusdorf, Anil Palepu, Chunjong Park, Jack W. O'Sullivan, Vishnu Ravi, Tim Strother, Pavel Dubov, Aliya Rysbek, Toshiyuki Fukuzawa, Yana Lunts, Jan Freyberg, Michael B. Chang, Aniruddh Raghu, David Stutz, Devora Berlowitz, Eliseo Papa, Taylan Cemgil, JD Velasquez, Jack Chen, Arthur Chen, Doug Fritz, Charlie Taylor, Katya Tregubova, Jing Rong Lim, Richard Green, Sara Mahdavi, Mahvish Nagda, Jihyeon Lee, Craig Schiff, Liviu Panait, Sukhdeep Singh, Valentin Liévin, David G. T. Barrett, Hannah Gladman, Anna Cupani, Francesca Pietra, Uchechi Okereke, Katherine Tong, Clemens Meyer, Erwan Rolland, Mili Sanwalka, Michael D. Howell, Shixiang Shane Gu, Bibo Xu, Euan A. Ashley, S. M. Ali Eslami, Gregory Wayne, Pushmeet Kohli, Vivek Natarajan, Adam Rodman, Alan Karthikesalingam, Ryutaro Tanno

The practice of medicine relies not only upon skillful dialogue but also on the nuanced exchange and interpretation of rich auditory and visual cues between doctors and patients. Building on the low-latency voice and video processing capabilities of Gemini, we introduce AI co-clinician, a first-of-its-kind conversational AI system utilizing continuous streams of audio-visual data from live patient conversations to inform real-time clinical decisions. Its dual-agent architecture balances deep clinical reasoning with the low latency required for natural dialogue. To assess this system, we implemented a video-based interface emulating telemedicine consultations. We crafted 20 standardized outpatient scenarios requiring proactive real-time auditory and visual reasoning and designed "TelePACES" evaluation criteria alongside case-specific rubrics. In a randomized, interface-blinded, crossover simulation study (n = 120 encounters) with 10 internal medicine residents as patient actors, we compared AI co-clinician with primary care physicians (PCPs), GPT-Realtime, and a baseline agent. AI co-clinician approached PCPs in key TelePACES dimensions, including management plans and differential diagnosis, while significantly outperforming GPT-Realtime across all general criteria. While our agent demonstrated parity with PCPs in case-specific triage measures, physicians maintained superior overall performance in case-specific assessments. Although AI co-clinician marks a significant advance in real-time telemedical AI, gaps remain in physical examination and disease-specific reasoning. Our work shows that text-only approaches fail to capture the true challenges of medical consultation and suggests that high-stakes real-time diagnostic AI is most safely advanced in collaborative, triadic models where AI can be a supportive co-clinician for doctors and patients.

摘要：醫學實踐不僅依賴於熟練的對話技巧，還依賴於醫生與患者之間豐富的聽覺和視覺線索的微妙交流與解釋。基於Gemini的低延遲語音和視頻處理能力，我們推出了AI共同醫生，這是一種首創的對話式AI系統，利用來自實時患者對話的連續音視頻數據來輔助即時臨床決策。其雙代理架構平衡了深度臨床推理與自然對話所需的低延遲。為了評估這一系統，我們實施了一個模擬遠程醫療諮詢的視頻介面。我們設計了20個標準化的門診場景，要求主動進行即時的聽覺和視覺推理，並設計了“TelePACES”評估標準以及特定案例的評分規範。在一項隨機、介面盲法的交叉模擬研究中（n = 120 次接觸），我們將AI共同醫生與初級保健醫生（PCPs）、GPT-Realtime和基準代理進行了比較，參與者為10名內科住院醫師擔任患者演員。AI共同醫生在關鍵的TelePACES維度上接近PCPs，包括管理計劃和鑑別診斷，同時在所有一般標準中顯著超越了GPT-Realtime。儘管我們的代理在特定案例的分診措施上與PCPs表現相當，但醫生在特定案例的評估中保持了優越的整體表現。雖然AI共同醫生標誌著實時遠程醫療AI的一次重大進展，但在身體檢查和疾病特定推理方面仍存在差距。我們的研究表明，僅依賴文本的方法無法捕捉醫療諮詢的真正挑戰，並建議高風險的實時診斷AI應在協作的三方模型中最安全地推進，在這種模型中，AI可以作為醫生和患者的支持共同醫生。

##### **Monocular Biomechanical Tracking of Fingers with Inverse Kinematics to Foundation Models**
2605.09258v1 by R. James Cotton, Pouyan Firouzabadi, Wendy Murray

Accurate hand and finger tracking from video has significant clinical applications for monitoring activities of daily living and measuring range of motion, yet monocular video approaches for obtaining hand biomechanics remain under-developed. We present a method that combines the SAM 3D Body foundation model with inverse kinematics optimization in a full-body biomechanical model to extract anatomically-constrained finger joint angles from single-view video. We port SAM 3D Body from PyTorch to JAX for integration with MuJoCo-MJX, enabling GPU-accelerated optimization, and develop a novel mapping between the Momentum Human Rig (MHR) outputs and biomechanical model markers. Validation against 8-camera multiview reconstruction on 4,590 frames from 7 participants performing a variety of hand poses and object manipulation tasks shows finger joint angle errors of approximately 10 degrees and hand position errors of approximately 6 mm, after Procrustes alignment. Results were consistent across camera viewpoints and robust to different methods for producing reference values from multiview video. This work extends monocular biomechanical analysis to detailed finger tracking, expanding access to quantitative characterization of hand movement from readily available video.

摘要：準確的手部和手指追蹤從視頻中具有重要的臨床應用，用於監測日常生活活動和測量運動範圍，然而，獲取手部生物力學的單眼視頻方法仍然發展不足。<lb/>我們提出了一種方法，將SAM 3D Body基礎模型與逆運動學優化相結合，建立一個全身生物力學模型，從單視角視頻中提取解剖學約束的手指關節角度。<lb/>我們將SAM 3D Body從PyTorch移植到JAX，以便與MuJoCo-MJX集成，實現GPU加速優化，並開發了一種新的映射，將Momentum Human Rig (MHR)的輸出與生物力學模型標記相連接。<lb/>對7名參與者在執行各種手部姿勢和物體操作任務時，從4,590幀的8攝像頭多視角重建進行的驗證顯示，手指關節角度誤差約為10度，手部位置誤差約為6毫米，經過Procrustes對齊後。<lb/>結果在不同攝像頭視角之間一致，並且對於從多視角視頻生成參考值的不同方法具有穩健性。<lb/>這項工作將單眼生物力學分析擴展到詳細的手指追蹤，擴大了從隨手可得的視頻中對手部運動的定量特徵描述的訪問。

##### **WavesFM: Hierarchical Representation Learning for Longitudinal Wearable Sensor Waveforms**
2605.09173v1 by Peng Cao, Zhijian Yang, Tennison Liu, Jonathan Wang, Jiang Wu, Magdalena Proszewska, Arvind Pillai, Mingwu Gao, Amir Farjadian, Lawrence Cai, Emily Blanchard, Daniel McDuff, Pramod Rudrapatna, Matthew Thompson, Anupam Pathak, Mark Malhotra, Shwetak Patel, Dina Katabi, Paolo Di Achille, Ming-Zher Poh

Wearable sensors enable the continuous acquisition of high-resolution physiological waveforms, such as photoplethysmography and accelerometry, under free-living conditions. However, inferring health-related phenotypes from these signals presents significant challenges due to high sampling frequencies, multimodal dependencies, and extreme sequence lengths (e.g., weeks of recordings), compounded by a scarcity of ground-truth labels. To address these challenges, existing self-supervised learning (SSL) methodologies typically follow two paradigms: (1) learning rich morphological representations from short waveform segments while collapsing longitudinal dynamics through simple aggregation, or (2) modeling behavioral patterns from coarse, hand-crafted features (e.g. heart rate, step counts) spanning longer horizons but foregoing subtle, predictive signatures in raw waveforms. To bridge this gap, we propose WavesFM, a foundation model utilizing a two-stage SSL framework for longitudinal physiological data. Specifically, we decompose the learning problem into two stages: first, a segment-level encoder is pretrained to extract local embeddings from short waveforms; subsequently, a temporal encoder is trained to model the sequence of these embeddings across a multi-day horizon. This hierarchical approach overcomes the computational complexity of high-resolution, long-sequence data, allowing the overall model to capture both local signal semantics and the complex circadian and inter-day variations governing physiological dynamics. Pretrained on over 6.8M hours (N=324k individuals) of recordings for the first stage and 5.3M hours (N=10k) for the second stage, WavesFM demonstrates superior performance across 58 diverse tasks spanning demographics, lifestyle, health conditions, and medications.

摘要：可穿戴傳感器使得在自由生活條件下持續獲取高解析度的生理波形成為可能，例如光電容積描記法和加速度計。然而，從這些信號中推斷與健康相關的表型面臨重大挑戰，這是由於高採樣頻率、多模態依賴性和極長的序列長度（例如，數週的錄音），再加上真實標籤的稀缺。為了解決這些挑戰，現有的自我監督學習（SSL）方法通常遵循兩種範式：（1）從短波形段學習豐富的形態表示，同時通過簡單的聚合來壓縮縱向動態，或（2）從粗略的手工特徵（例如心率、步數）建模行為模式，這些特徵涵蓋較長的時間範圍，但放棄了原始波形中的微妙預測特徵。為了填補這一空白，我們提出了WavesFM，一種利用兩階段SSL框架的基礎模型，用於縱向生理數據。具體而言，我們將學習問題分解為兩個階段：首先，對短波形進行預訓練的段級編碼器提取局部嵌入；隨後，訓練一個時間編碼器來建模這些嵌入在多天範圍內的序列。這種分層方法克服了高解析度、長序列數據的計算複雜性，使整體模型能夠捕捉局部信號語義以及支配生理動態的複雜晝夜和日間變化。在第一階段上預訓練了超過680萬小時（N=324k個個體）的錄音，第二階段則為530萬小時（N=10k），WavesFM在涵蓋人口統計、生活方式、健康狀況和藥物的58個多樣任務中展示了卓越的性能。

##### **Shapley Regression for Rare Disease Diagnosis Support: a case study on APDS**
2605.08897v1 by Safa Alsaidi, Tomás Brogueira, Nizar Mahlaoui, Marc Vincent, Guilherme Pelegrina, Nicolas Garcelon, Adrien Coulet, Miguel Couceiro

Activated PI3K8 Syndrome (APDS) is a rare genetic immune disorder caused by variants in PIK3CD or PIK3R1, with highly heterogeneous symptoms that often delay diagnosis. Early recognition is hampered by overlapping clinical presentations and limited clinician awareness, motivating systematic, data-driven approaches to detect APDS-associated phenotypic patterns in routine electronic health records. Traditional linear scoring systems cannot capture complex symptom interactions, while deep learning models, though expressive, often lack interpretability. To bridge this gap, we propose Shapley regression, a novel game-theoretic model replacing the linear predictor with a k-additive cooperative game, explicitly modeling co-occurrence of symptoms while maintaining the transparency and convexity of logistic regression. We carry out an empirical study of our lightweight method on eight public biomedical datasets, showing that a 2-additive model with $l_{2}$ regularization achieves an optimal trade-off between predictive power and noise robustness. We also apply it to a real-world cohort of 222 patients, on which Shapley regression accurately distinguished APDS cases from matched controls, confirming and validating phenotypes known to be associated with APDS, and facilitating the exploration of pairwise interactions between symptoms, validated by clinical experts.

摘要：啟動型 PI3K8 綜合症 (APDS) 是一種罕見的遺傳免疫疾病，由 PIK3CD 或 PIK3R1 的變異引起，具有高度異質的症狀，常常延遲診斷。<lb/>早期識別受到重疊臨床表現和醫生意識有限的阻礙，這促使我們採用系統性、數據驅動的方法來檢測 APDS 相關的表型模式在日常電子健康記錄中。<lb/>傳統的線性評分系統無法捕捉複雜的症狀互動，而深度學習模型雖然表達能力強，卻往往缺乏可解釋性。<lb/>為了彌補這一差距，我們提出了 Shapley 回歸，一種新穎的博弈論模型，用 k-additive 合作遊戲取代線性預測器，明確建模症狀的共現，同時保持邏輯回歸的透明性和凸性。<lb/>我們對我們的輕量級方法在八個公共生物醫學數據集上進行了實證研究，顯示出具有 $l_{2}$ 正則化的 2-additive 模型在預測能力和噪音穩健性之間達到了最佳平衡。<lb/>我們還將其應用於一個包含 222 名患者的真實世界隊列，Shapley 回歸準確地區分了 APDS 病例與匹配對照，確認並驗證了已知與 APDS 相關的表型，並促進了症狀之間的成對互動的探索，這得到了臨床專家的驗證。

##### **Geometrically Constrained Stenosis Editing in Coronary Angiography via Entropic Optimal Transport**
2605.08851v1 by Jialin Li, Zhuo Zhang, Yue Cao, Guipeng Lan, Jiabao Wen, Shuai Xiao, Jiachen Yang

The scarcity of high-quality imaging data for coronary angiography (CAG) stenosis limits the clinical translation of automated stenosis detection. Synthetic stenosis data provides a practical avenue to augment training sets, improving data quality, diversity, and distributional coverage, and enhancing detection precision and generalization. However, diffusion-based editing commonly relies on soft guidance in a noise-initialized reverse process, offering limited pixel-level precision and structure preservation. We propose the OT-Bridge Editor, which reframes localized editing as a constrained entropic optimal transport (OT) problem and leverages geometric information to steer the generation path, enabling stronger geometric control. Extensive experiments show that our synthesized angiograms consistently improve downstream stenosis detection, yielding substantial relative gains of 27.8% on the public ARCADE benchmark and 23.0% on our multi-center dataset, supported by consistent qualitative results.

摘要：高品質的冠狀動脈造影 (CAG) 狹窄影像數據稀缺，限制了自動狹窄檢測的臨床轉化。合成的狹窄數據提供了一種實用的途徑來增強訓練集，提高數據質量、多樣性和分佈覆蓋，並增強檢測精度和泛化能力。然而，基於擴散的編輯通常依賴於在噪聲初始化的反向過程中進行柔性引導，提供有限的像素級精度和結構保留。我們提出了OT-Bridge編輯器，將局部編輯重新框架為一個受限的熵最優傳輸 (OT) 問題，並利用幾何信息來引導生成路徑，實現更強的幾何控制。大量實驗表明，我們合成的血管造影圖在下游狹窄檢測中持續改善，公共ARCADE基準上獲得了27.8%的顯著相對增益，而在我們的多中心數據集中則達到23.0%，並且有一致的定性結果支持。

##### **Mental Health AI Safety Claims Must Preserve Temporal Evidence**
2605.08827v1 by Srimonti Dutta, Ratna Kandala

The safety of mental health AI is often judged at the wrong temporal scale. Current evaluations typically score isolated responses, endpoint outcomes, or aggregate dialogue quality, while clinically consequential failures may arise from the order and accumulation of interactions themselves, including delayed escalation, repeated reinforcement, dependency formation, failed repair, and gradual deterioration across turns. This paper argues that this mismatch is not merely a limitation of evaluation coverage but a source of invalid safety conclusions. We introduce Temporal Safety Non-Identifiability, a formal account of why safety properties that depend on sequence, timing, accumulation, or recovery cannot be certified by protocols that discard those features. From this formalization, we develop SCOPE (Safety Claims Over Preserved Evidence) as a general principle for aligning safety claims with the evidence an evaluation actually retains, and instantiate it as SCOPE-MH, a mental-health instantiation of this reporting standard. We operationalize SCOPE-MH through a proof-of-concept on the AnnoMI dataset of expert-annotated motivational interviewing conversations, which reveals mechanisms of failure that per-turn behavior scoring does not represent. We propose SCOPE-MH as a diagnostic complement to existing evaluation infrastructure and argue that evaluation preserving temporal evidence is necessary, not optional, for safety-critical mental health AI deployment.

摘要：心理健康人工智慧的安全性常常在錯誤的時間尺度上進行評估。當前的評估通常只針對孤立的反應、最終結果或綜合對話質量進行打分，而臨床上重要的失敗可能源於互動本身的順序和累積，包括延遲升級、重複強化、依賴形成、修復失敗以及在回合中的逐漸惡化。本文主張，這種不匹配不僅僅是評估範圍的局限性，而是一種無效安全結論的來源。我們引入了時間安全非可識別性，這是一個正式的說明，解釋了依賴於序列、時間、累積或恢復的安全性特徵為何無法通過忽略這些特徵的協議來認證。基於這一形式化，我們開發了SCOPE（基於保留證據的安全聲明）作為一個通用原則，用以將安全聲明與評估實際保留的證據對齊，並將其具體化為SCOPE-MH，這是一個心理健康報告標準的具體實現。我們通過對AnnoMI數據集的概念驗證來操作化SCOPE-MH，該數據集包含專家註釋的動機訪談對話，揭示了每回合行為評分未能表現的失敗機制。我們提出SCOPE-MH作為現有評估基礎設施的診斷補充，並主張保留時間證據的評估對於安全關鍵的心理健康人工智慧部署是必要的，而非可選的。

##### **Event Fields: Learning Latent Event Structure for Waveform Foundation Models**
2605.08685v1 by Li Na, Yuanyun Zhang, Shi Li

We propose a new class of waveform foundation models that departs from conventional sequence based representations by modeling physiological time series as realizations of latent event processes. Rather than treating signals as collections of local tokens or patches, our approach assumes that clinically meaningful structure arises from temporally extended, interacting events whose boundaries and dynamics are not directly observed. To capture this structure, we introduce a self supervised learning framework that enforces consistency across stochastic segmentations and time frequency projections of the same waveform, encouraging representations that are invariant to signal level perturbations while preserving event level organization. The resulting model combines a segmentation aware encoder with a latent interaction operator that captures dependencies among inferred events, and naturally extends to multimodal settings by aligning modalities through shared event representations. Across a range of physiological benchmarks, including arrhythmia classification, hemodynamic prediction, and waveform retrieval, the proposed method improves performance, robustness, and label efficiency relative to strong sequence based baselines. These results suggest that shifting from signal centric to event centric representations provides a more appropriate inductive bias for modeling physiological dynamics and offers a complementary path to scaling foundation models in healthcare.

摘要：我們提出了一種新的波形基礎模型類別，這種模型不同於傳統的基於序列的表示，通過將生理時間序列建模為潛在事件過程的實現來實現。<lb/>我們的方法假設臨床上有意義的結構源於時間上延伸的、相互作用的事件，這些事件的邊界和動態並不是直接觀察到的，而不是將信號視為局部標記或補丁的集合。<lb/>為了捕捉這種結構，我們引入了一個自我監督學習框架，該框架強制在相同波形的隨機分段和時間頻率投影之間保持一致性，鼓勵對信號級擾動不變的表示，同時保留事件級的組織。<lb/>最終模型結合了一個關注分段的編碼器和一個潛在交互運算符，該運算符捕捉推斷事件之間的依賴關係，並通過共享事件表示自然擴展到多模態設置。<lb/>在一系列生理基準測試中，包括心律失常分類、血流動力學預測和波形檢索，所提出的方法相對於強大的基於序列的基準提高了性能、穩健性和標籤效率。<lb/>這些結果表明，從以信號為中心轉向以事件為中心的表示為建模生理動力學提供了更合適的歸納偏見，並為在醫療保健中擴展基礎模型提供了一條互補的途徑。

##### **Explanation Fairness in Large Language Models: An Empirical Analysis of Disparities in How LLMs Justify Decisions Across Demographic Groups**
2605.08671v1 by Gautam Veldanda

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed not only to make decisions but to explain them. While AI decision fairness has been studied extensively, the fairness of AI explanations (whether LLMs justify decisions with equal quality, depth, tone, and linguistic sophistication across demographic groups) has received little attention. This paper introduces the Explanation Fairness Taxonomy (EFT), a framework comprising five formally defined, operationalizable dimensions: Verbosity Disparity, Sentiment Disparity, Epistemic Hedging Disparity, Decision-Linked Explanation Disparity, and Lexical Complexity Disparity. The taxonomy is instantiated in a controlled empirical study across 80 prompt templates, four consequential decision domains (hiring, medical triage, credit assessment, legal judgment), and five LLMs: GPT-4.1, Claude Sonnet, LLaMA 3.3 70B, GPT-OSS 120B, and Qwen3 32B. Two novel black-box metrics are introduced: the Hedging Density Score (HDS) and the Explanation Faithfulness Proxy (EFP), a heuristic indicator of decision-linked explanation variation. Across up to 400 prompt pairs, all eight EFT metrics show statistically significant disparities (Cohen's d ranging from small to large, all p_BH < 10^(-62)). Model choice is strongly associated with disparity magnitude: Qwen3 32B exhibits verbosity disparities 5.9x larger than LLaMA 3.3 70B. Two prompting-based mitigations show significant reductions in EFP disparity (78-95%) but no significant effect on stylistic dimensions, consistent with the hypothesis that stylistic explanation inequalities are encoded in pre-training distributions and are not resolvable through deployment-level instruction alone. A reproducible measurement framework is offered for explanation-level fairness auditing, with implications for AI regulation and deployment practice.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用來不僅做出決策，還解釋這些決策。儘管AI決策的公平性已經被廣泛研究，但AI解釋的公平性（即LLMs是否在不同人口群體中以相同的質量、深度、語調和語言複雜性來辯護決策）卻鮮有關注。本文介紹了解釋公平性分類法（EFT），這是一個由五個正式定義且可操作的維度組成的框架：冗長性差異、情感差異、認知對沖差異、決策相關解釋差異和詞彙複雜性差異。該分類法在一項控制的實證研究中具體化，涵蓋80個提示模板、四個重要的決策領域（招聘、醫療分診、信用評估、法律判決）和五個LLMs：GPT-4.1、Claude Sonnet、LLaMA 3.3 70B、GPT-OSS 120B和Qwen3 32B。引入了兩個新穎的黑箱指標：對沖密度分數（HDS）和解釋忠實性代理（EFP），這是一個決策相關解釋變異的啟發式指標。在多達400對提示中，所有八個EFT指標顯示出統計上顯著的差異（Cohen's d範圍從小到大，所有p_BH < 10^(-62)）。模型選擇與差異大小有強烈關聯：Qwen3 32B的冗長性差異是LLaMA 3.3 70B的5.9倍。兩種基於提示的緩解措施顯示EFP差異顯著減少（78-95%），但對風格維度沒有顯著影響，這與假設一致，即風格解釋的不平等是在預訓練分佈中編碼的，並且僅通過部署層級的指令無法解決。提供了一個可重複的測量框架，用於解釋層級的公平性審核，對AI的監管和部署實踐具有重要意義。

##### **PromptDx: Differentiable Prompt Tuning for Multimodal In-Context Alzheimer's Diagnosis**
2605.08585v1 by Lujia Zhong, Yihao Xia, Shuo Huang, Jianwei Zhang, Yonggang Shi

Deep learning models in medical imaging typically operate as parametric memory, diagnosing patients by recalling fixed knowledge learned during training. This contrasts sharply with clinical practice, where physicians employ analogical reasoning to diagnose new cases by referencing similar records from past exemplars. While In-Context Learning (ICL) frameworks such as Tabular Prior-Fitted Networks (TabPFN) offer a promising diagnosis-by-reference paradigm, they are designed with tabular-specific inductive priors and rely on non-differentiable preprocessing pipelines, leading to manifold mismatch and gradient fracture when applied to heterogeneous multimodal data. To address these limitations, we propose PromptDx, a novel diagnosis-by-reference framework that leverages a pre-trained TabPFN as an ICL engine while enabling seamless integration with multimodal representations. Our core contribution is a Differentiable Prompt Tuning (DPT) mechanism that aligns a Masked Multimodal Modeling module with the pre-trained ICL engine. By training a lightweight adapter as a differentiable surrogate for the engine's non-differentiable preprocessors, we enable an end-to-end optimization of multimodal prompts within the ICL paradigm. We validate our method on the Alzheimer's Disease Neuroimaging Initiative (ADNI) dataset using 3D MRI and tabular biomarkers. Experiments demonstrate that our approach outperforms traditional parametric baselines. Notably, our method achieves superior performance using only 1% context samples compared to 30% in standard ICL, demonstrating exceptional manifold condensation ability. We further validate the generalizability of our DPT framework across six tabular datasets with diverse scales. Overall, our method offers a more data-efficient and clinically aligned paradigm for Alzheimer's Disease diagnosis.

摘要：深度學習模型在醫學影像中通常作為參數化記憶運作，通過回憶訓練期間學習的固定知識來診斷患者。這與臨床實踐形成鮮明對比，醫生通過參考過去範例的相似記錄來進行類比推理以診斷新病例。儘管像表格先驗擬合網絡（TabPFN）這樣的上下文學習（ICL）框架提供了一種有前景的參考診斷範式，但它們是以特定於表格的歸納先驗設計的，並依賴於不可微分的預處理管道，這在應用於異質多模態數據時會導致流形不匹配和梯度斷裂。為了解決這些限制，我們提出了PromptDx，一種新穎的參考診斷框架，利用預訓練的TabPFN作為ICL引擎，同時實現與多模態表示的無縫集成。我們的核心貢獻是一種可微調提示（DPT）機制，將一個掩蔽多模態建模模塊與預訓練的ICL引擎對齊。通過訓練一個輕量級適配器作為引擎不可微分預處理器的可微分替代，我們實現了在ICL範式中對多模態提示的端到端優化。我們在阿茲海默病神經影像倡議（ADNI）數據集上使用3D MRI和表格生物標記驗證我們的方法。實驗表明，我們的方法超越了傳統的參數基準。值得注意的是，我們的方法在僅使用1%的上下文樣本時達到了優越的性能，而標準ICL則需要30%，顯示出卓越的流形凝聚能力。我們進一步驗證了我們的DPT框架在六個具有不同規模的表格數據集上的可泛化性。總體而言，我們的方法為阿茲海默病診斷提供了一種更具數據效率和臨床對齊的範式。

##### **Human-LLM Dialogue Improves Diagnostic Accuracy in Emergency Care**
2605.08533v1 by Burcu Sayin, Ngoc Vo Hong, Ipek Baris Schlicht, Jacopo Staiano, Pasquale Minervini, Sara Allievi, Nicola Susca, Nicola Osti, Alberto Maino, Vito Racanelli, Andrea Passerini

Clinical decision-making in emergency medicine demands rapid, accurate diagnoses under uncertainty. Despite benchmark progress, evidence for LLMs as interactive aids in live physician workflows remains sparse. MedSyn lets physicians iteratively query an LLM provided with the full clinical record while initially viewing only the chief complaint. Seven physicians (three seniors, four residents) completed baseline and AI-assisted sessions across 52 MIMIC-IV cases stratified by difficulty. Blinded evaluation showed residents' Hard-case correctness rose from 0.589 to 0.734; difficulty-standardised completely-correct rates confirmed a medium effect (Δ = 0.092; p = 0.071; d = 0.47). Automated metrics corroborated these gains: standardised any-match accuracy improved by 0.156 (p < 0.0001), and residents showed the largest F1 gain (Δ = 0.138; p < 0.0001). Dialogue analysis revealed expertise-dependent strategies (seniors asked targeted, hypothesis-driven questions; residents relied on broader queries) and cross-expertise concordance increased (Δ = 0.145; p < 0.0001). Interactive LLM support meaningfully enhances diagnostic reasoning.

摘要：臨床決策在急診醫學中要求在不確定性下迅速、準確地進行診斷。儘管在基準進展方面取得了一定成就，但有關大型語言模型（LLMs）作為實時醫生工作流程中的互動輔助工具的證據仍然稀少。MedSyn 讓醫生在最初僅查看主要抱怨的情況下，反覆查詢提供完整臨床記錄的 LLM。七位醫生（三位高年級醫生，四位住院醫師）在52個根據難度分層的 MIMIC-IV 案例中完成了基線和 AI 輔助會議。盲評顯示住院醫師在難題的正確率從 0.589 上升至 0.734；難度標準化的完全正確率確認了中等效應（Δ = 0.092；p = 0.071；d = 0.47）。自動化指標證實了這些增益：標準化的任意匹配準確率提高了 0.156（p < 0.0001），住院醫師顯示出最大的 F1 增益（Δ = 0.138；p < 0.0001）。對話分析揭示了依賴專業知識的策略（高年級醫生提出針對性的、假設驅動的問題；住院醫師依賴更廣泛的查詢），並且跨專業的一致性增加（Δ = 0.145；p < 0.0001）。互動式 LLM 支持顯著增強了診斷推理。

##### **AI-Care: A Conversational Agentic System for Task Coordination in Alzheimer's Disease Care**
2605.08480v1 by Preyash Yadav, Michelle Cohn, Priyanka Koppolu, Hritvik Agarwal, Amey Gohil, Tejas Patil, Sasha Pimento, Alyssa Weakley

Individuals with Alzheimer's disease (AD) and Alzheimer's disease-related dementia (ADRD) experience memory and thinking changes that impact their ability to use digital daily management tools. For example, adding an event to a digital calendar requires multiple steps that may act as barriers to independent use for individuals with AD/ADRD. This paper presents AI-Care, a conversational agentic artificial intelligence (AI) layer built on top of a remote caregiving platform co-designed with people with AD/ADRD. AI-Care is designed to reduce the cognitive load on individuals with AD/ADRD when managing everyday tasks such as setting calendar reminders and organizing to-do lists through natural-language interaction with a voice-first chatbot. The system uses a LangGraph-based stateful orchestration approach in which each request passes through sanitization, intent classification, context loading, safety checks, deterministic slot collection, tool execution, and response composition. Safety-critical responses, particularly around medications and allergies, are grounded in caregiver-verified records rather than free-form model generation. The system does not make autonomous medical or treatment decisions. Incomplete or ambiguous requests are handled through controlled multi-turn clarification rather than silent failure or guessing. The system supports both typed and spoken input, with voice output through ElevenLabs text-to-speech. Longer responses are chunked before synthesis to avoid rushed playback. A preliminary pilot with four individuals with mild-to-moderate AD/ADRD showed that users found the system trustworthy, competent, and likable, and were able to complete the evaluated coordination tasks through conversation. We describe the design goals, system architecture, safety controls, and findings from this formative evaluation.

摘要：患有阿茲海默症 (AD) 和與阿茲海默症相關的癡呆症 (ADRD) 的個體經歷記憶和思維的變化，這影響了他們使用數位日常管理工具的能力。<lb/>例如，將事件添加到數位日曆需要多個步驟，這可能成為AD/ADRD患者獨立使用的障礙。<lb/>本文介紹了AI-Care，這是一個建立在與AD/ADRD患者共同設計的遠端照護平台之上的對話式代理人工智慧 (AI) 層。<lb/>AI-Care旨在減輕AD/ADRD患者在管理日常任務（如設置日曆提醒和組織待辦事項清單）時的認知負擔，透過與以語音為主的聊天機器人的自然語言互動來實現。<lb/>該系統使用基於LangGraph的狀態管理編排方法，其中每個請求經過清理、意圖分類、上下文加載、安全檢查、確定性槽位收集、工具執行和響應組合。<lb/>安全關鍵的響應，特別是有關藥物和過敏的部分，基於護理人員驗證的記錄，而不是自由形式的模型生成。<lb/>該系統不會做出自主的醫療或治療決策。<lb/>不完整或模糊的請求通過受控的多輪澄清處理，而不是靜默失敗或猜測。<lb/>該系統支持輸入的打字和語音，並通過ElevenLabs的文本轉語音技術提供語音輸出。<lb/>較長的響應在合成之前會被分塊，以避免播放過快。<lb/>對四位輕度至中度AD/ADRD患者進行的初步試點顯示，用戶認為該系統值得信賴、能力強且令人喜愛，並能夠通過對話完成評估的協調任務。<lb/>我們描述了設計目標、系統架構、安全控制以及這次形成性評估的發現。

##### **Measuring What Matters: Benchmarking Generative, Multimodal, and Agentic AI in Healthcare**
2605.08445v1 by Prasanna Desikan, Harshit Rajgarhia, Shivali Dalmia, Ananya Mantravadi

AI models are increasingly deployed in live clinical environments where they must perform reliably across complex, high-stakes workflows that standard training and validation datasets were never designed to capture. Evaluating these systems requires benchmarks: structured combinations of tasks, datasets, and metrics that enable reproducible, comparable measurement of what a model can do. The central challenge in healthcare AI is not performance alone, but the absence of systematic methods to measure reliability, safety, and clinical relevance under real-world conditions. Most existing benchmarks test what a model knows; too few test whether it can perform reliably and without failing across the full complexity of real clinical tasks. Current benchmarks have accumulated through ad hoc dataset construction optimized for narrow task performance: frontier models achieve near-perfect scores on medical licensing examinations, but when evaluated across real clinical tasks, performance degrades sharply, scoring 0.74--0.85 on documentation, 0.61--0.76 on clinical decision support, and only 0.53--0.63 on administrative and workflow tasks \cite{medhelm}. High benchmark scores give a false sense of deployment readiness, and the gap between performance and utility widens precisely as AI systems take on more consequential clinical roles. Without a principled framework for benchmark design, the field cannot determine whether poor clinical performance reflects model limitations or failures in how performance is being measured.

摘要：AI 模型越來越多地應用於實際臨床環境中，在這些環境中，它們必須在複雜、高風險的工作流程中可靠地執行，而標準的訓練和驗證數據集從未設計用來捕捉這些情況。評估這些系統需要基準：結構化的任務、數據集和指標的組合，使得對模型能做什麼進行可重複、可比較的測量。醫療保健 AI 的核心挑戰不僅是性能，還在於缺乏系統的方法來測量在現實條件下的可靠性、安全性和臨床相關性。大多數現有的基準測試模型所知的內容；而能否在真實臨床任務的全部複雜性中可靠地執行且不失敗的測試則太少。當前的基準是通過為狹窄任務性能優化的臨時數據集構建而積累的：前沿模型在醫學執照考試中獲得近乎完美的分數，但在真實臨床任務中評估時，性能急劇下降，在文檔上得分 0.74--0.85，在臨床決策支持上得分 0.61--0.76，而在行政和工作流程任務上僅得分 0.53--0.63 \cite{medhelm}。高基準分數給人一種錯誤的部署準備感，而性能與實用性之間的差距正是隨著 AI 系統承擔更重要的臨床角色而擴大。沒有一個原則性的基準設計框架，該領域無法確定不佳的臨床性能是反映模型的局限性還是性能測量方式的失敗。

##### **MPD$^2$-Router: Mask-aware Multi-expert Prior-regularized Dual-head Deferral Router in Glaucoma Screening and Diagnosis**
2605.08024v1 by Wenxin Zhan

Learning-to-defer (L2D) can make glaucoma screening safer by routing difficult/uncertain cases to humans, yet standard formulations overlook expert availability, heterogeneous readers behavior, workload imbalance, asymmetric diagnostic harm, case difficulty from morphology and deployment shift. We introduce MPD$^2$-Router, a mask-aware multi-expert deferral framework that recasts ophthalmic triage as constrained human--AI routing: whether to defer and to which available expert. It couples a dual-head deferral/allocation policy with mask-aware Gumbel--sigmoid gating that strictly enforces per-sample availability, and fuses uncertainty, morphology, image-quality, and OOD signals. Training uses an asymmetric cost-sensitive objective with an augmented-Lagrangian deferral budget, a group-specific distribution prior, and a rank-majorization JS regularizer that jointly prevent expert collapse without forcing uniform allocation. Across three cross-national glaucoma cohorts (REFUGE, CHAKSU, ORIGA) with a frozen REFUGE-trained backbone, MPD$^2$-Router substantially lowers clinical cost and improves MCC over AI-only at a moderate deferral rate. It is Pareto-optimal in F1--MCC--cost, robust under cross-domain shift, and yields balanced expert utilization.

摘要：學習延遲 (L2D) 可以透過將困難/不確定的案例轉交給人類來使青光眼篩檢更安全，然而標準的公式忽略了專家的可用性、異質的讀者行為、工作負載不平衡、不對稱的診斷傷害、形態學帶來的案例難度以及部署轉變。我們介紹了 MPD$^2$-Router，一個具備掩碼感知的多專家延遲框架，將眼科分診重新詮釋為受限的人類--AI 路由：是否延遲以及轉交給哪位可用專家。它將雙頭延遲/分配政策與掩碼感知的 Gumbel--sigmoid 閘結合，嚴格執行每個樣本的可用性，並融合不確定性、形態學、圖像質量和 OOD 信號。訓練使用不對稱的成本敏感目標，搭配增強拉格朗日延遲預算、特定群體的分佈先驗，以及一個排名最大化的 JS 正則化器，這些共同防止專家崩潰而不強迫均勻分配。在三個跨國青光眼隊列 (REFUGE、CHAKSU、ORIGA) 中，使用一個凍結的 REFUGE 訓練骨幹，MPD$^2$-Router 顯著降低臨床成本，並在中等延遲率下改善 MCC，相較於僅使用 AI 的情況。它在 F1--MCC--成本上是帕累托最優的，對跨領域轉變具有穩健性，並實現了平衡的專家利用率。

##### **FQPDR: Federated Quantum Neural Network for Privacy-preserving Early Detection of Diabetic Retinopathy**
2605.08324v1 by Debashis De, Mahua Nandy Pal, Dipankar Hazra

Diabetic Retinopathy (DR) is a common complication of diabetes that can lead to blindness of people. Detecting DR at the earliest stage is essential to prevent irreversible eye damage. Microaneurysm dots are the first signs of DR. As the dots are tiny and of low contrast, detecting mild DR is a very challenging task. Federated learning (FL) preserves data privacy, which is a major concern for medical image processing. FL is a collaborative learning method, which shares only the model parameters with a server, without sharing the patient data to a central server. Inspired by classical FL, we propose a federated learning-based quantum neural network (federated QNN) for this task. We implemented the models with limited samples and few learnable parameters from the E-ophtha and Retina MNIST datasets. The crossevaluation efficiency of the proposed federated quantum neural network system for privacy-preserving early detection of diabetic retinopathy (FQPDR) in Kaggle dataset images indicates the robustness of the light weight learning models. FQPDR performances are inspiring while considering existing non-FL and FL methods.

摘要：糖尿病視網膜病變（DR）是糖尿病的一種常見併發症，可能導致人們失明。<lb/>在最早的階段檢測DR對於防止不可逆的眼部損傷至關重要。<lb/>微動脈瘤點是DR的第一個跡象。<lb/>由於這些點很小且對比度低，檢測輕度DR是一項非常具有挑戰性的任務。<lb/>聯邦學習（FL）保護數據隱私，這是醫學影像處理的一個主要關注點。<lb/>FL是一種協作學習方法，只與伺服器共享模型參數，而不將患者數據共享到中央伺服器。<lb/>受到經典FL的啟發，我們提出了一種基於聯邦學習的量子神經網絡（聯邦QNN）來處理這一任務。<lb/>我們在E-ophtha和Retina MNIST數據集上實現了有限樣本和少量可學習參數的模型。<lb/>所提出的聯邦量子神經網絡系統在Kaggle數據集圖像中進行隱私保護的糖尿病視網膜病變早期檢測（FQPDR）的交叉評估效率表明了輕量級學習模型的穩健性。<lb/>考慮到現有的非FL和FL方法，FQPDR的表現令人鼓舞。

##### **TimeLesSeg: Unified Contrast-Agnostic Cross-Sectional and Longitudinal MS Lesion Segmentation via a Stochastic Generative Model**
2605.07955v1 by Vicent Caselles-Ballester, Eloy Martínez-Heras, Giuseppe Pontillo, Zoe Mendelsohn, Elena M. Marrón, Juan Luis García Fernández, Laia Subirats, Jon Stutters, Jeremy Chataway, Frederik Barkhof, Sara Llufriu, Ferran Prados

Multiple sclerosis (MS) expresses substantial clinical and radiological heterogeneity, which poses significant challenges for automatic lesion segmentation. The current deep learning-based SOTA is highly susceptible to changes in both distribution, e.g., changes in scanner; as well as the structure of inputs, evident in the current divide between cross-sectional and longitudinal approaches. We introduce TimeLesSeg, a unified contrast-agnostic framework designed to segment MS lesions regardless of the presence of a temporal dimension in its inputs, with a single convolutional neural network. Our approach models pathological priors through lesion masks, which are processed together with the current scan. Cross-sectional processing is enabled by exposing the model to training cases where no prior information is available, which are modeled with an empty mask, allowing it to operate seamlessly in both scenarios. To overcome the scarcity and inconsistency of longitudinal datasets, we propose a novel generative pipeline in which patterns of lesion evolution are simulated by stochastically deforming each individual lesion with morphological operations, producing realistic prior timepoints. In parallel, we achieve contrast agnosticism through Gaussian mixture model-based domain randomization, enabling the network to experience a wide spectrum of intensity profiles. Results on three publicly available and two in-house datasets show that TimeLesSeg outperforms the contrast-agnostic state of the art on single-modality inputs across overlap- and distance-based metrics. In longitudinal processing, our method outperforms SAMSEG, and captures lesion load dynamics more accurately than both the former and LST-AI. All source code related to the development of TimeLesSeg is available at https://github.com/NeuroADaS-Lab/TimeLesSeg.

摘要：多發性硬化症（MS）表現出顯著的臨床和放射學異質性，這對自動病變分割提出了重大挑戰。當前基於深度學習的最先進技術對於分佈的變化（例如，掃描儀的變化）以及輸入結構的變化高度敏感，這在當前橫斷面和縱向方法之間的區分中顯而易見。我們引入了TimeLesSeg，一個統一的無關對比框架，旨在使用單一卷積神經網絡分割MS病變，無論其輸入中是否存在時間維度。我們的方法通過病變掩模建模病理先驗，這些掩模與當前掃描一起處理。通過將模型暴露於沒有先前信息的訓練案例來實現橫斷面處理，這些案例用空掩模建模，使其能夠在兩種情境中無縫運作。為了克服縱向數據集的稀缺性和不一致性，我們提出了一個新穎的生成管道，其中通過隨機變形每個個別病變並進行形態學操作來模擬病變演變的模式，產生現實的先前時間點。同時，我們通過基於高斯混合模型的領域隨機化實現了對比無關性，使網絡能夠體驗到廣泛的強度配置文件。在三個公開可用和兩個內部數據集上的結果顯示，TimeLesSeg在基於重疊和距離的指標上超越了單模態輸入的對比無關最先進技術。在縱向處理中，我們的方法超越了SAMSEG，並比前者和LST-AI更準確地捕捉病變負荷動態。與TimeLesSeg開發相關的所有源代碼可在 https://github.com/NeuroADaS-Lab/TimeLesSeg 獲得。

##### **BeeVe: Unsupervised Acoustic State Discovery in Honey Bee Buzzing**
2605.07903v1 by Hamze Hammami, Nidhal Abdulaziz

Discovering structure in biological signals without supervision is a fundamental problem in computational intelligence, yet existing bioacoustic methods assume vocal production models or predefined semantic units, leaving non-vocal species poorly served. This work introduces BeeVe, an unsupervised framework for acoustic state discovery in collective honey bee buzzing. BeeVe uses the self-supervised Patchout Spectrogram Transformer (PaSST) as a frozen feature extractor, then trains a Vector-Quantized Variational Autoencoder (VQ-VAE) without labels on those embeddings, learning a finite discrete codebook of acoustic tokens directly from unlabelled hive audio. No labels, pretext tasks, or contrastive objectives are used at any stage. Post-hoc evaluation against known queen status reveals that the learned tokens separate queenright and queenless conditions with Jensen-Shannon Divergence values between 0.609 and 0.688, and that the queenless condition further decomposes into three internally coherent sub-states stable across experiments with different codebook sizes and random seeds. Token transition analysis confirms non-random sequential structure (p << 0.001) across all experiments. Generalisation to unseen recordings preserves both token overlap (Jaccard = 0.947) and global manifold topology. These results demonstrate that unsupervised discrete codebook learning can recover repeatable acoustic structure from a non-vocal biological signal without annotation, opening a path toward non-invasive acoustic hive health monitoring.

摘要：發現生物信號中的結構而不需監督是一個計算智能中的基本問題，然而現有的生物聲學方法假設了聲音產生模型或預定義的語義單元，導致非聲音物種的服務不足。這項工作介紹了BeeVe，一個用於集體蜜蜂嗡嗡聲的無監督聲音狀態發現框架。BeeVe使用自我監督的Patchout Spectrogram Transformer (PaSST)作為凍結的特徵提取器，然後在這些嵌入上無標籤地訓練向量量化變分自編碼器（VQ-VAE），直接從未標記的蜂巢音頻中學習有限的離散聲音代碼本。任何階段都不使用標籤、前提任務或對比目標。針對已知的女王狀態進行的事後評估顯示，學習到的代碼在女王在和女王缺失條件之間以Jensen-Shannon Divergence值在0.609和0.688之間分離，且女王缺失的條件進一步分解為三個在不同代碼本大小和隨機種子實驗中穩定的內部一致子狀態。代碼轉換分析確認了所有實驗中非隨機的序列結構（p &lt;&lt; 0.001）。對未見錄音的泛化保留了代碼重疊（Jaccard = 0.947）和全局流形拓撲。這些結果證明無監督的離散代碼本學習可以從非聲音生物信號中恢復可重複的聲音結構而無需註釋，為非侵入式的蜂巢健康監測開闢了一條道路。

##### **Approximation-Free Differentiable Oblique Decision Trees**
2605.07837v1 by Subrat Prasad Panda, Blaise Genest, Arvind Easwaran

Decision Trees (DTs) are widely used in safety-critical domains such as medical diagnosis, valued for their interpretability and effectiveness on tabular data. However, training accurate oblique DTs is challenging due to complex optimization landscapes and overfitting risks, particularly in regression. Recent advances have introduced differentiable formulations that enable gradient-based training and joint optimization of decision boundaries and leaf regressors. Yet, existing approaches typically rely on approximations, either through probabilistic softening of boundaries (soft DTs) or quantized gradients such as the Straight-Through Estimator (STE). To overcome these limitations, we propose DTSemNet, a novel, semantically equivalent, and invertible representation of hard oblique DTs as neural networks. DTSemNet enables end-to-end training with standard gradient descent, eliminating the need for approximations in both classification and regression. While classification aligns naturally with this formulation, regression remains challenging due to the joint optimization of internal nodes and leaf regressors. To address this, we analyze the limitations of STE and introduce an annealed Top-k method that provides accurate gradient signals without approximation. Extensive experiments on classification and regression benchmarks show that DTSemNet-trained oblique DTs outperform state-of-the-art differentiable DTs. Furthermore, we demonstrate that DTSemNet can serve as programmatic DT policies in reinforcement learning environments, thereby broadening their applicability.

摘要：決策樹（DTs）廣泛應用於醫療診斷等安全關鍵領域，因其可解釋性和對表格數據的有效性而受到重視。<lb/>然而，由於複雜的優化地形和過擬合風險，訓練準確的斜決策樹是一項挑戰，特別是在回歸中。<lb/>最近的進展引入了可微分的公式，使得基於梯度的訓練和決策邊界及葉回歸器的聯合優化成為可能。<lb/>然而，現有的方法通常依賴於近似，無論是通過邊界的概率軟化（軟決策樹）還是量化梯度，例如直通估計器（STE）。<lb/>為了克服這些限制，我們提出了DTSemNet，一種新穎的、語義等價的、可逆的硬斜決策樹表示形式，作為神經網絡。<lb/>DTSemNet使得標準梯度下降的端到端訓練成為可能，消除了在分類和回歸中對近似的需求。<lb/>雖然分類與這一公式自然對應，但由於內部節點和葉回歸器的聯合優化，回歸仍然具有挑戰性。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們分析了STE的限制，並引入了一種退火Top-k方法，該方法提供準確的梯度信號而無需近似。<lb/>在分類和回歸基準上的大量實驗表明，經過DTSemNet訓練的斜決策樹超越了最先進的可微分決策樹。<lb/>此外，我們還展示了DTSemNet可以作為強化學習環境中的程序性決策樹策略，從而擴大其適用性。

##### **GNN for Structural Displacement Prediction**
2605.08303v1 by Hung-Fu Chang, Tzu-Kang Lin, Yung-Li Cheng

Accurate prediction of structural displacements under external loading is fundamental to structural health monitoring and seismic safety assessment. Although the finite element method (FEM) remains the prevailing approach because of its high accuracy, its considerable computational cost restricts its suitability for real-time monitoring applications. To address this limitation, this study proposes a data-driven framework based on Graph Neural Networks (GNNs), in which structural systems are represented as graphs with joints modeled as nodes and structural members as edges. By incorporating both geometric and mechanical properties into the graph representation, the proposed model learns the relationship between applied loads and structural responses directly from simulated data. A synthetic dataset was generated from a two-story frame structure using ANSYS, and both a conventional Neural Network (NN) and a GNN were trained for comparison. The results show that the proposed GNN framework predicts displacements and rotations with high accuracy and outperforms the NN model, demonstrating its potential as a fast and efficient alternative to traditional FEM-based analysis.

##### **SGC-RML: A reliable and interpretable longitudinal assessment for PD in real-world DNS**
2605.08302v1 by Wenbin Wei, Ruixiang Gao, Suyuan Yao, Xuanzhen Zhao, Cheng Huang, Hen-Wei Huang

Real-world digital Parkinson's disease assessment faces challenges such as heterogeneous modalities, cross-device bias, and incomplete labeling. Existing methods often focus on average predictive performance, lacking the reliability mechanisms needed for retrospective reliability-aware assessment - namely, determining when the model is reliable, when to reject an assessment, when to retest, and from which symptom dimensions the predictions are based. This paper proposes SGC-RML, which maps speech, gait, wearable motion, mobility tasks, and clinical variables to a shared 8-dimensional symptom node space (7 clinical symptom nodes and 1 reliability_state auxiliary node), unifying motor and non-motor representations through a symptom atlas. By jointly introducing uncertainty estimation, conformal calibration, and selective decision routing, the model can not only predict symptoms and severity but also reject assessments or suggest retests when evidence is insufficient. We validate this framework on five real-world PD datasets, covering classification, regression, event detection, and longitudinal severity prediction. Experiments show that SGC-RML achieves an MAE of 4.579 / R^2 of 0.772 on PPMI, an AUC of 0.953 on mPower, and an AUC of 0.825 on PADS. Under leak-free temporal anchoring, as few as 5 subject-specific anchors transform UCI from an essentially non-predictive subject-independent setting (motor MAE 8.38, CCC 0.02) into a calibrated longitudinal assessment (motor MAE 3.24, CCC 0.756) with split-conformal coverage held at the 0.80 target. Under the Daphnet LOSO protocol, it achieves an F1 of 0.803 / AUC of 0.872. These results demonstrate that SGC-RML provides a unified paradigm for accurate, calibrated, auditable, and symptom-interpretable retrospective longitudinal assessment of PD under incomplete multimodal conditions.

摘要：現實世界中的數位帕金森病評估面臨著異質性模式、跨設備偏差和標記不完整等挑戰。現有的方法通常專注於平均預測性能，缺乏進行回顧性可靠性評估所需的可靠性機制——即確定模型何時可靠、何時拒絕評估、何時重新測試，以及預測基於哪些症狀維度。本文提出了SGC-RML，該模型將語音、步態、可穿戴運動、移動任務和臨床變量映射到一個共享的8維症狀節點空間（7個臨床症狀節點和1個可靠性狀態輔助節點），通過症狀圖譜統一運動和非運動表徵。通過共同引入不確定性估計、符合性校準和選擇性決策路由，該模型不僅可以預測症狀和嚴重程度，還可以在證據不足時拒絕評估或建議重新測試。我們在五個真實世界的PD數據集上驗證了這一框架，涵蓋了分類、回歸、事件檢測和縱向嚴重程度預測。實驗顯示，SGC-RML在PPMI上達到了4.579的MAE / 0.772的R^2，在mPower上達到了0.953的AUC，在PADS上達到了0.825的AUC。在無洩漏的時間錨定下，僅需5個特定於受試者的錨點即可將UCI從基本上無法預測的受試者獨立設置（運動MAE 8.38，CCC 0.02）轉變為經過校準的縱向評估（運動MAE 3.24，CCC 0.756），並保持分裂符合性覆蓋在0.80的目標下。在Daphnet LOSO協議下，該模型達到了0.803的F1 / 0.872的AUC。這些結果表明，SGC-RML為在不完整多模態條件下準確、經過校準、可審計和可解釋的PD回顧性縱向評估提供了一個統一的範式。

##### **A Paired Point-of-Care Ultrasound Dataset for Image Quality Enhancement and Benchmarking via a cGAN Baseline**
2605.08282v1 by Lennard M. van Karnenbeek, Hilde G. A. van der Pol, Mark Wijkhuizen, Eva Poelman, Caroline A. Drukker, Theo Ruers, Freija Geldof, Behdad Dashtbozorg

Purpose: We aim to enhance the image quality of point-of-care ultrasound (POCUS) devices using deep learning and a novel paired dataset of POCUS and high-end ultrasound images.
  Approach: We collected the first accurately paired dataset using a custom-built automated gantry system of low-end POCUS and high-end ultrasound images. A conditional generative adversarial network (cGAN) was utilized based on the pix2pix architecture, with a U-Net generator that incorporates both L1 and structural similarity index (SSIM) losses to improve perceptual quality. Pretraining on a simulation dataset further boosts performance. Evaluation was performed on 1064 paired ex vivo tissue and phantom ultrasound image sets.
  Results: Our approach improves the SSIM from 0.29 to 0.54 and PSNR from 19.16 dB to 22.41 dB. No-reference metrics also indicate substantial enhancement, with the Natural Image Quality Evaluator (NIQE) and Perception-based Image Quality Evaluator (PIQE) scores dropping from 7.95 to 4.44 and 31.12 to 19.99, respectively.
  Conclusions: This work presents the first publicly available accurately paired dataset of low-end POCUS to high end ultrasound images. Additionally, our results demonstrate the potential of the proposed framework to overcome hardware limitations of handheld POCUS, enhancing its diagnostic value in low-resource and point-of-care settings. The POCUS-IQ Dataset is publicly available at https://github.com/NKI-MedTech-AI/POCUS-IQ.
